[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing session using LLVM’s libFuzzer detected a heap-use-after-free in the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystemd network link parser. AddressSanitizer reports that memory freed by [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`condition_free` is subsequently accessed in `condition_free_list_type`, leading to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man invalid read. The issue manifests when running the `fuzz-link-parser` harness on[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma crafted testcase.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue: During fuzzing of the network link configuration parser, AddressSanitizer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflags a “heap-use-after-free” at `condition.[0m[1;92mc:100:9[0m[39m` inside the function [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`condition_free_list_type`. Memory previously freed by `condition_free` is later [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread, causing undefined behavior.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type: Heap use-after-free [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUAF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash stack trace begins in `condition_free_list_type` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcondition.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miterates over a freed linked list.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The list nodes are allocated by `condition_new` and freed in `condition_free`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The free happens as part of parsing network conditions in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`config_parse_net_condition` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnet-condition.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, invoked by the generic [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`conf-parser.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzz harness calls `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, which in turn calls [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`link_load_one` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlink-config.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to parse and then free link configuration [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructures.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer output shows the exact allocation and free stack frames, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirming the UAF.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to examine:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/shared/condition.c` — implementations of `condition_new`, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`condition_free`, and `condition_free_list_type`.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/shared/net-condition.c` — function `config_parse_net_condition` where [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditions are parsed and freed.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/shared/conf-parser.c` — generic parsing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`next_assignment`, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parse_line`, `config_parse_many`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/udev/net/link-config.c` — entry points `link_load_one` and [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`link_config_free` that wrap the parsing and cleanup.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fuzz-link-parser.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m — triggers the code path under test but is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot itself the root cause.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/basic/list.h:[0m[1;36m190[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m209[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m190[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m_p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m                                                 \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m191[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mLIST_REMOVE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, *_a, _p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;                     \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:                _p;                                                     \[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35mLIST_CLEAR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, head, free_func[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m       \[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35m_LIST_CLEAR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, head, free_func, [0m[1;35mUNIQ_T[0m[1;39m([0m[39melem, UNIQ[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* Clear the list, destroying each element with free_func *[0m[35m/[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35m_LIST_CLEAR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, head, free_func, elem[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m        \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m{[0m[39m                                              \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m201[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mtypeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhead[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m elem;                      \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m202[0m[39m:                while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39melem = [0m[1;35mLIST_POP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, head[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m   \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m203[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mfree_func[0m[1;39m([0m[39melem[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;                \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m204[0m[39m:                head;                                   \[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m205[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m206[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m207[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* Now include [0m[32m"macro.h"[0m[39m, because we want our definition of [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmacros above use. We include[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m208[0m[39m: * it down here instead of up top, since macro.h pulls in log.h which in turn [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeds our own definitions. *[0m[35m/[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m209[0m[39m:#include [0m[32m"macro.h"[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function condition_free_list_type iterates over a linked list of Condition[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnodes via LIST_FOREACH, calling [0m[1;35mcondition_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on matching nodes without [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munlinking them.  Since [0m[1;35mcondition_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply frees the node’s memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia mfree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut does not update its neighbors’ pointers, the LIST_FOREACH loop will [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequently dereference freed memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39myielding UAF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the list head remains a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdangling pointer.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A second symptom is that in link-config.c, the call to clear the [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlist—[0m[1;35mcondition_free_list[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconfig->conditions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m—does not capture the returned [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mupdated[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m head pointer, so even after proper unlink-&-free, config->conditions [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains a stale [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdangling[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pointer.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Principles to Preserve[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing parsing logic in config_parse_net_condition relies on [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcondition_free_list_type returning the new list head, which is assigned back to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*list.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No fuzz-harness or test code modifications; only shared library source files.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintain final behavior: dropping old conditions of a given type before adding[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew ones, or clearing all when rvalue is empty.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Outline[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Revise condition_free_list_type in src/shared/condition.c[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the LIST_FOREACH + [0m[1;35mcondition_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unlinked‐free pattern with safe [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munlinking via LIST_REMOVE before freeing.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leverage LIST_CLEAR for “clear all” [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtype < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to reuse existing idioms that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munlink each node before invoking a free function.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After clearing or type‐filtered removals, return the updated head pointer so [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat callers can resynchronize their list head.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   New pseudocode for condition_free_list_type:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Condition* [0m[1;35mcondition_free_list_type[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCondition *head, ConditionType type[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         Condition *c, *next;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtype < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Unlink & free every node[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mLIST_CLEAR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconditions, head, condition_free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39m!head[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m list should now be empty[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return head;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Remove only matching nodes[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc = head; c; c = next[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             next = c->conditions_next;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc->type == type[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mLIST_REMOVE[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconditions, head, c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mcondition_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtype >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m non‐negative type leaves any non‐matching nodes [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintact[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return head;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     · No freed node remains in the list during iteration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno use‐after‐free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     · The head pointer variable [0m[1;39m([0m[39minside the function[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is updated correctly as [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnodes at the head are unlinked.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     · Callers reassign their list head from the return value.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Fix call site in src/udev/net/link-config.c[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - change from:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```c[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mcondition_free_list[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconfig->conditions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     to:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```c[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       config->conditions = [0m[1;35mcondition_free_list[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconfig->conditions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rationale: unlike config_parse_net_condition [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich does `*list = [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcondition_free_list_type[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, link_config_free invoked condition_free_list but [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mignored its return. We must reassign config->conditions to the [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnow possibly NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhead, preventing a dangling field.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In src/shared/condition.c:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate condition_free_list_type [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m92[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace its body with the safe‐unlink implementation shown above, using [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLIST_CLEAR for type<[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m and a for‐loop plus LIST_REMOVE for type ≥ [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Retain the existing signature and the final [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtype ≥ [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || !head[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In src/udev/net/link-config.c:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - On the line where [0m[1;35mcondition_free_list[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconfig->conditions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is called, prefix[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit with `config->conditions =`.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Rebuild and re-run the fuzz‐link‐parser harness under AddressSanitizer to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm the UAF is resolved and no new memory or logic regressions occur.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unlinking before free matches existing LIST_CLEAR logic in basic/list.h, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving list discipline and eliminating UAF.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returning and reassigning the new head pointer ensures no stray dangling [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointers remain in config structures.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing parsing and cleanup flows reassign or capture the returned head, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving the intended “drop‐old‐conditions” semantics without altering harness or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If any code assumed `condition_free_list_type` would leave `head` untouched on[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpartial removals, that assumption no longer holds. However, callers in the codebase[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mconfig_parse_net_condition, link_config_free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m always immediately overwrite their [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`*list` or `config->conditions` from the return value, so behavior is consistent.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broad exception catching is introduced; error paths unchanged.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change to harness, no modifications to external dependencies, and existing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munit tests or integration tests remain valid.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References in Codebase[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The LIST_CLEAR macro in src/basic/list.h already illustrates safe [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munlink‐and‐free patterns.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - config_parse_net_condition correctly reassigns its `*list` from the return of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcondition_free_list_type. We mirror that discipline in link-config.c.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
